   218	{

   239	void FretDiagram::updateDiagram(const String& harmonyName)
   240	{
   241	    std::vector<DiagramInfo> availableDiagrams = patternsFromHarmony(harmonyName);
   242	    if (availableDiagrams.empty()) {
   243	        return;
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    String diagramXml = resolveDiagram(availableDiagrams).diagramXml;
   247	
   248	    if (diagramXml.empty()) {
   249	        return;
   250	    }
   251	
   252	    clear();
   253	
   254	    read460::ReadContext ctx;
   255	    XmlReader reader(diagramXml.toUtf8());
   256	
   257	    read460::TRead::read(this, reader, ctx);
   258	
   259	    triggerLayout();
   260	    return;
   261	}

   263	double FretDiagram::mainWidth() const
   264	{
   265	    double mainWidth = 0.0;
   266	    if (orientation() == Orientation::VERTICAL) {
   267	        mainWidth = ldata()->stringDist * (strings() - 1);
   268	    } else if (orientation() == Orientation::HORIZONTAL) {
   269	        mainWidth = ldata()->fretDist * frets();
   270	    }
   271	    return mainWidth;
   272	}

   286	
   287	void FretDiagram::setStrings(int n)
   288	{
   289	    int difference = n - m_strings;
   290	    if (difference == 0 || n <= 0) {
   291	        return;
   292	    }
   293	
   294	    // Move all dots, makers, barres to the RIGHT, so we add strings to the left
   295	    // This is more useful - few instruments need strings added to the right.
   296	    DotMap tempDots;
   297	    MarkerMap tempMarkers;
   298	
   299	    for (int string = 0; string < m_strings; ++string) {
   300	        if (string + difference < 0) {
   301	            continue;
   302	        }
   303	
   304	        for (auto const& d : dot(string)) {
   305	            if (d.exists()) {
   306	                tempDots[string + difference].push_back(FretItem::Dot(d));
   307	            }
   308	        }
   309	
   310	        if (marker(string).exists()) {

   701	        if (!barrePart.startsWith(u'B')) {
   702	            continue;
   703	        }
   704	
   705	        size_t lb = barrePart.indexOf(u'[');
   706	        size_t rb = barrePart.indexOf(u']');
   707	        if (lb < 2 || rb < lb) {
   708	            continue;
   709	        }
   710	
   711	        int fret = barrePart.mid(1, lb - 1).toInt();
   712	        if (fret <= 0) {
   713	            continue;
   714	        }
   715	
   716	        String range = barrePart.mid(lb + 1, rb - lb - 1);
   717	        size_t dash = range.indexOf('-');
   718	        if (dash > 0) {
   719	            int start = range.left(dash).toInt();
   720	            int end = range.mid(dash + 1).toInt();
   721	            if (start >= 0 && end >= start && end < stringCount) {
   722	                diagram->setBarre(start, end, fret - offset);
   723	            }
   724	        }
   725	    }

   727	
   728	String FretDiagram::patternFromDiagram() const
   729	{
   730	    const int diagramStrings = strings();
   731	    const int offset = fretOffset();
   732	
   733	    StringList patternParts;
   734	    const DotMap& dotsMap = dots();
   735	
   736	    for (int i = 0; i < diagramStrings; ++i) {
   737	        const FretItem::Marker fretMarker = marker(i);
   738	
   739	        if (fretMarker.mtype == FretMarkerType::CROSS) {
   740	            patternParts.push_back(u"X");
   741	            continue;
   742	        } else if (fretMarker.mtype == FretMarkerType::CIRCLE) {
   743	            patternParts.push_back(u"O");
   744	            continue;
   745	        }
   746	
   747	        const auto it = dotsMap.find(i);
   748	        std::vector<FretItem::Dot> dotList;
   749	        if (it != dotsMap.end()) {
   750	            const std::vector<FretItem::Dot>& dots = it->second;
   751	            for (const FretItem::Dot& dot : dots) {
   752	                if (!dot.isPartOfSlurBarre) { // Don't write dot if part of slur barré
   753	                    dotList.push_back(dot);
   754	                }
   755	            }
   756	        }
   757	
   758	        if (!dotList.empty()) {
   759	            const auto& dotList2 = it->second;
   760	            StringList dotDescriptions;
   761	            for (const auto& dot : dotList2) {
   762	                if (dot.isPartOfSlurBarre) {
   763	                    continue;
   764	                }
   765	
   766	                int actualFret = dot.fret + offset;
   767	                Char typeChar = u'O';
   768	
   769	                switch (dot.dtype) {
   770	                case FretDotType::NORMAL:   typeChar = u'O';
   771	                    break;
   772	                case FretDotType::CROSS:    typeChar = u'X';
   773	                    break;
   774	                case FretDotType::SQUARE:   typeChar = u'S';
   775	                    break;
   776	                case FretDotType::TRIANGLE: typeChar = u'T';
   777	                    break;
   778	                default: break;
   779	                }
   780	
   781	                dotDescriptions.push_back(String::number(actualFret) + u'-' + typeChar);
   782	            }
   783	
   784	            patternParts.push_back(u'[' + dotDescriptions.join(u",") + u']');
   785	        } else {
   786	            patternParts.push_back(u"-");
   787	        }
   788	    }
   789	
   790	    String pattern = patternParts.join(u"");
   791	
   792	    const BarreMap& _barres = barres();
   793	    StringList barreParts;
   794	    for (const auto& [fret, b] : _barres) {
   795	        if (!b.exists()) {
   796	            continue;
   797	        }
   798	
   799	        int adjustedFret = fret + offset;
   800	        int start = b.startString;
   801	        int end = (b.endString != -1) ? b.endString : diagramStrings - 1;
   802	
   803	        barreParts.push_back(u'B' + String::number(adjustedFret)
   804	                             + u'[' + String::number(start)
   805	                             + u'-' + String::number(end) + u']');
   806	    }
   807	
   808	    if (!barreParts.empty()) {
   809	        pattern += u';' + barreParts.join(u";");
   810	    }
   811	
   812	    return pattern;
   813	}
   814	
   815	std::vector<String> FretDiagram::harmoniesFromPattern(const String& pattern) const

   817	    if (s_diagramPatternToHarmoniesMap.empty()) {
   818	        readHarmonyToDiagramFile(HARMONY_TO_DIAGRAM_FILE_PATH);
   819	    }
   820	    return muse::value(s_diagramPatternToHarmoniesMap, pattern);

   822	
   823	std::vector<DiagramInfo> FretDiagram::patternsFromHarmony(const String& harmonyName)
   824	{

   826	        readHarmonyToDiagramFile(HARMONY_TO_DIAGRAM_FILE_PATH);

  1364	bool FretDiagram::isCustom(const String& harmonyNameForCompare) const
  1365	{
  1366	    if (harmonyNameForCompare.empty()) {
  1367	        return false;
  1368	    }
  1369	
  1370	    static constexpr std::array props {
  1371	        Pid::FRET_STRINGS,
  1372	        Pid::FRET_FRETS,
  1373	        Pid::FRET_NUT,
  1374	        Pid::FRET_FINGERING
  1375	    };
  1376	
  1377	    for (const Pid& pid : props) {
  1378	        if (pid == Pid::FRET_FINGERING) {
  1379	            if (custom(Pid::FRET_SHOW_FINGERINGS)) {
  1380	                return true;
  1381	            }
  1382	        } else if (custom(pid)) {
  1383	            return true;
  1384	        }
  1385	    }
  1386	
  1387	    if (s_harmonyToDiagramMap.empty()) {
  1388	        readHarmonyToDiagramFile(HARMONY_TO_DIAGRAM_FILE_PATH);
  1389	    }
  1390	
  1391	    NoteSpellingType spellingType = style().styleV(Sid::chordSymbolSpelling).value<NoteSpellingType>();
  1392	    HarmonyMapKey key = createHarmonyMapKey(harmonyNameForCompare, spellingType, score()->chordList());
  1393	
  1394	    std::vector<DiagramInfo> availableDiagrams = muse::value(s_harmonyToDiagramMap, key);
  1395	    if (availableDiagrams.empty()) {
  1396	        return true;
  1397	    }
  1398	
  1399	    String currentPattern = patternFromDiagram();
  1400

  1402	        if (diagram.diagramPattern == currentPattern) {
  1403	            return false;
  1404	        }
  1405	    }
  1406	
  1407	    return true;
  1408	}

cat > /tmp/reproduce_fret_diagrams.py <<'PY'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
from pathlib import Path
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

xml_path = Path('/testbed/src/engraving/data/harmony_to_diagram.xml')
root = ET.parse(xml_path).getroot()

expected = {
    'em7': 'O[2-O][2-O]O[3-O]O',
    'dm7': 'XXO[2-O][1-O][1-O]',
}

actual = {}
for harmony_to_diagram in root.findall('HarmonyToDiagram'):
    name_el = harmony_to_diagram.find('./Harmony/name')
    pattern_el = harmony_to_diagram.find('pattern')
    if name_el is not None and pattern_el is not None and name_el.text in expected:
        actual[name_el.text] = pattern_el.text

ok = True
for name, expected_pattern in expected.items():
    pattern = actual.get(name)
    print(f'{name}: {pattern} (expected {expected_pattern})')
    if pattern != expected_pattern:
        ok = False

raise SystemExit(0 if ok else 1)
PY

import struct,zlib
for fn in ['/tmp/primg0.png','/tmp/primg1.png']:
    data=open(fn,'rb').read(); pos=8; chunks=[]; idat=b''
    while pos<len(data):
        ln=struct.unpack('>I',data[pos:pos+4])[0]; typ=data[pos+4:pos+8]; dat=data[pos+8:pos+8+ln]; pos+=12+ln
        chunks.append((typ,ln))
        if typ==b'IHDR': print(fn,'IHDR',struct.unpack('>IIBBBBB',dat))
        if typ==b'IDAT': idat+=dat
    print(chunks[:10], 'idat',len(idat), 'decomp',len(zlib.decompress(idat)))
PY

-rw-r--r-- 1 root root   7134 May  9 07:19  parse_mscx.py
from lxml import etree as ET
import argparse
import copy

def extract_fret_harmony_pairs(mscx_path):
    tree = ET.parse(mscx_path)
    root = tree.getroot()

    elements = []

    for fret in root.iter("FretDiagram"):
        harmony = fret.find("Harmony")
        if harmony is not None:
            elements.append(fret)
            elements.append(harmony)

    pairs = []
    i = 0
    while i < len(elements) - 1:
        if elements[i].tag == "FretDiagram" and elements[i + 1].tag == "Harmony":
            pairs.append((elements[i], elements[i + 1]))
            i += 2
        elif elements[i].tag == "Harmony" and elements[i + 1].tag == "FretDiagram":
            pairs.append((elements[i + 1], elements[i]))
            i += 2
        else:
            i += 1

    return pairs

def remove_barre_overlapping_dots(fret_elem, offset):
    strings = fret_elem.findall("string")

    for barre in fret_elem.findall("barre"):
        start = int(barre.get("start", -1))
        end = int(barre.get("end", -1))
        fret = int(barre.text.strip()) + offset

        for string in strings:
            string_no = int(string.get("no", -1))
            dot = string.find("dot")
            if dot is not None and start <= string_no <= end:
                dot_fret = int(dot.get("fret", -1)) + offset
                if dot_fret == fret:
                    string.remove(dot)

def extract_pattern_from_fretdiagram(fret_elem):
    strings_count = 6
    offset_elem = fret_elem.getparent().find("fretOffset")
    offset = int(offset_elem.text) if offset_elem is not None else 0

    pattern = ['-' for _ in range(strings_count)]
    barre_parts = []

    for string_elem in fret_elem.findall("string"):
        string_no = int(string_elem.get("no", -1))
        if not (0 <= string_no < strings_count):
            continue

        marker = string_elem.find("marker")
        dot_elems = string_elem.findall("dot")
        dot_descriptions = []

        if marker is not None and not dot_elems:
            marker_type = marker.text.strip().lower()
            if marker_type == "cross":
                pattern[string_no] = "X"
            elif marker_type == "circle" or marker_type == "o":
                pattern[string_no] = "O"

        elif dot_elems:
            for dot_elem in dot_elems:
                fret = int(dot_elem.get("fret", -1))
                dot_type = dot_elem.text.strip().lower() if dot_elem.text else "normal"

                type_char = "O"
                if dot_type == "cross":
                    type_char = "X"
                elif dot_type == "square":
                    type_char = "S"
                elif dot_type == "triangle":
                    type_char = "T"

                if fret >= 0:
                    dot_descriptions.append("%d-%s" % (fret + offset, type_char))

            if dot_descriptions:
                pattern[string_no] = "[" + ",".join(dot_descriptions) + "]"

    for barre_elem in fret_elem.findall("barre"):
        start = int(barre_elem.get("start", -1))
        end = int(barre_elem.get("end", -1))
        barre_fret_text = barre_elem.text.strip()

        if not barre_fret_text.isdigit() or not (0 <= start < strings_count):
            continue

        if end == -1:
            end = strings_count - 1
        if end < start or end >= strings_count:
            continue

        barre_fret = int(barre_fret_text) + offset

        for i in range(start, end + 1):
            current = pattern[i]
            if current.startswith("[") and current.endswith("]"):
                inner = current[1:-1]
                new_inner = []
                for dot_str in inner.split(","):
                    parts = dot_str.strip().split("-")
                    if len(parts) != 2:
                        continue
                    try:
                        fret_val = int(parts[0])
                    except ValueError:
                        continue
                    if fret_val != barre_fret:
                        new_inner.append(dot_str)
                if new_inner:
                    pattern[i] = "[" + ",".join(new_inner) + "]"
                else:
                    pattern[i] = "-"
            elif current == str(barre_fret):
                pattern[i] = "-"

        barre_parts.append("B%d[%d-%d]" % (barre_fret, start, end))

    base_pattern = ''.join(pattern)
    if barre_parts:
        base_pattern += ';' + ';'.join(barre_parts)

    return base_pattern

def get_harmony_name(harmony_elem):
    name_elem = harmony_elem.find("name")
    return name_elem.text.strip().lower() if name_elem is not None and name_elem.text else "unknown"

def build_output_xml(pairs):
    data_elem = ET.Element("Data")

    for fret_elem, harmony_elem in pairs:
        name = get_harmony_name(harmony_elem)

        htd = ET.SubElement(data_elem, "HarmonyToDiagram")
        fret_diagram_elem = ET.SubElement(htd, "FretDiagram")

        for child in fret_elem:
            if child.tag == "eid" or child.tag == "Harmony":
                continue
            elif child.tag == "fretDiagram":
                fret = copy.deepcopy(child)

                offset_elem = fret_elem.getparent().find("fretOffset")
                offset = int(offset_elem.text) if offset_elem is not None else 0
                remove_barre_overlapping_dots(fret, offset)

                fret_diagram_elem.append(fret)

                pattern = extract_pattern_from_fretdiagram(fret)
                pattern_elem = ET.SubElement(htd, "pattern")
                pattern_elem.text = pattern

            elif child.tag == "string" and fret_elem.find("fretDiagram") is not None and child not in fret_elem.find("fretDiagram"):
                continue
            else:
                fret_diagram_elem.append(copy.deepcopy(child))

        harmony_out = ET.SubElement(htd, "Harmony")
        name_elem = ET.SubElement(harmony_out, "name")
        name_elem.text = name

    return data_elem

def indent(elem, level=0):
    i = "\n" + level * "    "
    if len(elem):
        if not elem.text or not elem.text.strip():
            elem.text = i + "    "
        for child in elem:
            indent(child, level + 1)
        if not elem[-1].tail or not elem[-1].tail.strip():
            elem[-1].tail = i
    if level and (not elem.tail or not elem.tail.strip()):
        elem.tail = i
    return elem

def main():
    # Example: python2 parse_mscx.py --in "/path/to/file.mscx" --out /path/to/result.xml
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Extract Harmony and FretDiagram pairs from .mscx and output XML.")
    parser.add_argument('--in', dest='input_file', required=True, help='Path to the input .mscx file')
    parser.add_argument('--out', dest='output_file', required=True, help='Path to the output .xml file')
    args = parser.parse_args()

    pairs = extract_fret_harmony_pairs(args.input_file)
    root_elem = build_output_xml(pairs)
    indent(root_elem)

    tree = ET.ElementTree(root_elem)
    tree.write(args.output_file, encoding="utf-8", xml_declaration=True)

    print("Finished")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
